Vincent Broman http : //www.znet.com/~broman/ This version of the bible is encoded conformant to level 1 specifications of the Corpus Encoding Standard .
The English is to serve as the base for the parallel corpus , which will include aligned versions of the text in different languages .
Corpus Encoding Standard , Version 2.0 Marked up to the level of chapter and verse .
